Information Officer</span></div></td><td colspan="3" style="border-bottom:1pt solid #000000;border-top:1pt solid #000000;padding:2px 1pt;text-align:center;vertical-align:top"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">90%</span></td></tr></table></div><div><span style="color:#ffffff;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">TIP payouts will be </span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">2024 TIP payouts will continue to be primarily determined by the Company's 2024 performance on two key financial performance metrics: operating income (40%) and Systemwide sales (30%), which include sales at all restaurants, whether operated by the Company or by franchisees. In addition to the financial metrics, 2024 TIP payouts for the named executive officers listed above will include a metric measuring new restaurant openings (15%) and a strategic scorecard (15%) which will measure leadership&#8217;s efforts on several strategic initiatives. </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Each of these metrics is viewed as a critical driver of the Company&#8217;s success. </span></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt">Operating income is a key component of the Company&#8217;s strategy because it requires the Company to balance increases in revenue with financial discipline to produce strong margins.</span></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt">Systemwide sales is important in our franchise model because income generation is closely correlated to sales growth and is a good measure of franchisee health given our large percentage of franchised restaurants.</span></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt">New restaurant openings measures a key component of the Company&#8217;s </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accelerating the Arches</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> growth strategy.</span></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt">The strategic scorecard will measure leadership&#8217;s efforts on key initiatives including the Company&#8217;s franchising strategy, employee engagement, and diversity, equity and inclusion.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The financial metrics and new restaurant openings are measured on a consolidated or business segment level basis, as applicable to each individual. For Messrs. Borden, Kempczinski and Rice, and for Ms. Ralls-Morrison, the payout will be based on (i) consolidated financial performance (operating income and Systemwide sales); (ii) the number of new restaurant openings for both the McDonald&#8217;s USA and International Operated Markets business segments (together, the &#8220;Corporate Openings&#8221;); and (iii) a qualitative evaluation of the Company&#8217;s performance related to the initiatives reflected on the strategic scorecard. For Mr. Erlinger, the payout will be based on (i) a combination of McDonald&#8217;s USA and consolidated financial performance (operating income and Systemwide sales); (ii) the number of new restaurant openings for McDonald&#8217;s USA and the Corporate Openings; and (iii) a qualitative evaluation of the Company&#8217;s performance related to the initiatives reflected on the strategic scorecard.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The payout factor for 2024 TIP awards for all the above individuals can range from zero to a maximum of 200% of the target award. </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For compensation purposes, performance results may be adjusted from those reported in our financial statements in order to focus our executives on the fundamentals of the Company&#8217;s underlying business performance. For example, results are expressed in constant currencies to neutralize the impact of foreign currency translation.</span></div><div style="height:45pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><span><br/></span></div></div></div><div id="i569b691209014c52a17e24e62a9a38f0_10"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:45pt;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div><div style="text-align:center"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New
